\centering%
\setbox0=\hbox{%
\parbox{0.95\cardinnerwidth}{%
  \vspace{5pt}%
  \setstretch{0.8}%
  \fontsize{9}{10}\selectfont%
  \mbox{ル}, \mbox{ロ} \\[2pt]%
  \mbox{じ}, \mbox{みち} \\[2pt]%

  \vspace*{\fill}\\[0pt]%
  \hspace*{\fill}\rule[0pt]{0.2\cardinnerwidth}{0.5pt}\hspace*{\fill}%

  \hspace*{\fill}\rule[0pt]{0.2\cardinnerwidth}{0.5pt}\hspace*{\fill}\\[0pt]%
  \vspace*{\fill}%
  \fontsize{8}{9}\selectfont%
  \begin{multicols}{2}[]%
    %up to 6 compound meanings like '    \item [hiragana] [translation]'
    \begin{enumerate}[leftmargin=13pt,itemsep=1pt,parsep=2pt,topsep=2pt,partopsep=2pt,font=\normalfont\small]%
\item どうろ\\*

\item ろじょう\\*

\item しんろ\\*

\item こうそくどうろ\\*
autoroute, voie express
\item せんろ\\*
rail, voie ferrée, ligne de chemin de fer\\
\end{enumerate}%
  \end{multicols}%
  \vspace*{\fill}%
}%
}%

\box0

}
\end{flashcard}
